we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .	我們擔心從andeanridge北部運過來的可卡因
we worry about the movement of illegal weapons and trafficking . above all , perhaps , we worry about human trafficking , and the awful cost of it .	我們擔心非法武器的運行和販賣 。 最重要的是 , 我們擔心人口販賣 , 以及它的糟糕代價 。
trafficking moves largely at sea but in other parts of the global commons .	大部分的人口販賣是在海上遷移 , 但在全球公有物的其他地方 。
this is a photograph , and i wish i could tell you that this is a very hightech piece of us navy gear that we're using to stop the trafficking .	這是一張照片 , 我希望我能告訴你們這是美國海軍一個非常高科技的裝備 , 我們用它來阻止人口販賣 。
the bad news is , this is a semisubmersible run by drug cartels .	壞消息是 , 這是一個販毒集團的半潛水器
it was built in the jungles of south america .	在南美洲的叢林中被建造出來 。
we caught it with that lowtech raft — — and it was carrying six tons of cocaine .	我們用那個低科技的筏子逮到它 , 它帶著六噸的可卡因 。
crew of four . sophisticated communications sweep .	四個船員 , 精密的溝通都掃過了 ,
this kind of trafficking , in narcotics , in humans , in weapons , god forbid , in weapons of mass destruction , is part of the threat to the global commons .	這種販賣 , 在毒品、在人身上、在武器上、上帝禁止使用大規模毀滅性武器 , 是全球公有物的威脅之一 。
and let's pull it together in afghanistan today .	讓我們一起在今天的阿富汗 。
this is a field of poppies in afghanistan .	這是在阿富汗的一片乾草田
eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	全世界80%到90%的貘 , 鴉片和海洛因是從阿富汗出來的
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	我們也會看到 , 當然 , 恐怖主義
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	這就是基地組織的由來 。
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到了一股強烈的暴動深植在那兒 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以 , 這種恐怖主義也是全球公有物的一部分 , 我們必須要處理的是什麼 。
so here we are , 21st century .	所以 , 在21世紀 ,
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道我們的20世紀工具是行不通的 。
what should we do ?	我們應該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我認為我們不能僅僅依靠槍支來遞送安全 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不能僅僅依靠槍支來遞送安全 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們需要軍事力量的應用 。
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們著手進行時 , 我們必須表現得很好 , 而且要有能力 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但我的論點是 , 開放式安全是關乎國際的 , 跨部門的 , 私人的和公共的聯系 , 由互聯網上策略性溝通的想法聚集在一起 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我舉幾個例子來說明這如何以一個正向的角度運作
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 。 這些是阿富汗士兵 。
they are all holding books .	他們都拿著書 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說: 「 真奇怪 。 我想我讀到在這個人口 , 二十幾到三十幾歲的年輕男女在阿富汗是不識字的 。 」
you would be correct .	你會是正確的 。
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	85%的人進入阿富汗的安全部隊時無法閱讀 。
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為什麼 ? 因為塔利班的教育 , 在這段時間裡 , 這些男女都學會了閱讀 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那裡拿著書 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在教導他們讀書 , 在北約組織課程 , 和私營機構合作 , 和發展機構合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們已經教了超過二十萬名阿富汗安全部隊士兵 , 讓他們基本上能讀和寫 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你可以在阿富汗閱讀和寫作時 , 你通常會在你的口袋裡放一支筆 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	在畢業典禮上 , 當這些年輕男女畢業時 , 他們很驕傲地拿下那筆 , 放進他們的口袋裡 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	這也帶來國際組織 , 有50個國家參與這項任務-跨部門-開發機構和私人公共事務來進行這樣的安全 。
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	當然 , 我們也在教導他們對抗技能 , 但我認為 , 開放式安全意味著用能創造更持久的安全的方式來連結 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國海軍戰艦 。
it's called the comfort .	叫做舒適感
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一艘叫默西的姊妹船
they are hospital ships .	他們是醫院的船隻
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這個 , 舒適的 , 在加勒比海及南美洲的海岸操作 , 進行病人的治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	在典型的巡迴演出中 , 他們會進行40萬個病人治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	船員不是被軍隊嚴格對待 , 而是被人道主義組織合併:希望、專案微笑 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織送來志願者
interagency physicians come out .	跨部門的醫師走出來
they're all part of this .	它們都是這部分的一部分 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	給你一個例子 , 這個小男孩 , 8歲 , 跟著他的母親走了兩天來到安慰號的眼科診所 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他靈光乍現時 , 他突然抬頭說 , " mama , veoelmundo. "
" mom , i see the world . "	「 媽 , 我看到世界了 。 」
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	把這個乘以40萬的病患治療 , 這個私人和公共的合作以安全力量進行 , 你就會開始看到以截然不同的方式創造安全的力量 。
here you see baseball players .	這裡你看到的是棒球選手
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能在這張照片中挑出兩名美國軍人嗎 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是兩位年輕男孩兩邊的年輕人 。 這是棒球診所的一部分 , 我們在那兒探索了棒球聯盟棒球聯賽 , 國務院設立了外交部 , 棒球選手 , 他們是真正的戰士 , 他們參與了這個任務 , 他們在拉丁美洲和加勒比地區 , 宏都拉斯和加勒比地區 , 開到了所有中美洲和加勒比的棒球 , 開到了所有美洲 , 開到了賽道上 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它向年輕男女展示了關于健身和生活的榜樣 , 我主張協助為我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	這個合作的另一方面是災難救援 。
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是美國空軍的直升機參加2004年的海嘯殺死25萬人
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在所有這些重大災難中2004年海嘯 , 250 , 000死 , 2005年巴基斯坦的喀什米里地震 , 85000死 , 海地地地震 , 300 , 000死 , 更近期就是那些駭人聽聞的地震海嘯雙重打擊日本和其核能產業在所有這些例子中 , 我們看到了國際間 , 跨部門 , 私結合的合作 , 促進了安全的發展 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	所以這些都是關於公開資源安全的例子
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們將它綁在一起 , 逐漸地 , 藉由像這樣的東西 ,
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	現在 , 你看到這個想法: 「 啊 , 馬達 , 這些一定是通信電纜 , 或者這些可能是光纖電纜 。 」
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不是的 。 這是twitter編輯的世界地圖 。
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫色是推特 , 綠色是地緣 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是綜合體 。
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	這是個完美的避免人口普查 , 六個世界最大的國家依次排序:中國、印度、臉書、美國、推特和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	為什麼我們會想要拿到這些網子 ?
why do we want to be involved ?	我們為什麼想參與 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們之前談到阿拉伯之春 , 以及這一切的力量 。
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我再舉一個例子 , 就是你如何移動這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦的一段時間做這樣的演講 。 我對你們說 , 我在臉書上 。 朋友 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	得到聽眾的小笑聲 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	有一篇文章是ap , 在電線上執行 。
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	被世界上兩個地方接起來:芬蘭和印尼 。
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	標題是:北約艦隊司令需要好友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	故事是催化劑 , 隔天早上 , 我有數百個facebook朋友請求 , 來自印尼和芬蘭人 , 大多是說: 「 司機 , 我們聽說你需要一個朋友 , 哦 , 順帶一提 , nato是甚麼 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	是啊 , 我們笑了 , 但這就是我們如何移動訊息 , 而這個訊息就是我們如何連結國際 , 跨部門 , 私人和公共事業 , 還有這些社交網路來協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 讓我用一個嚴肅的語調
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這是一張勇敢的英國士兵的照片 。
he's in the scots guards .	他在蘇格蘭衛隊
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他站在helmand的手錶上 , 在阿富汗南部 。
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我把他放在這裡來提醒我們 , 我不會希望任何人離開房間 , 認為我們沒有能力 , 沒有能力 , 沒有能力 , 能夠創造真正的軍事效果 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	這就是我們是誰的核心 , 我們所做的事是為了保護自由 , 言論自由 , 所有我們在社會中珍視的東西 。
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但 , 你知道 , 人生不是一個開關 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要有一支隊伍 , 不是在戰鬥中 , 就是在戰場上 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我主張生命是一種恩典 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你得把它撥進去 , 在我看來 , 我們在這21世紀如何創造安全的時候 , 有些時候 , 我們會在真正的戰爭和危機中使用真正的權力 , 但會有許多的例子 , 如我們今天談過的 , 我們的軍隊能夠參與創造21世紀安全 , 國際 , 跨部門 , 公私結合 , 以能力交流 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	在結束前 , 我想說我們今天聽到的主題是關於維基百科 。 我經常使用維基百科查一些事實 , 正如你們所有人所理解的 , 維基百科並不是由12個聰明的人鎖定在一個房間寫文章而產生的 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科 , 每天都有成千上萬的人在輸入資訊 , 而每一天有數百萬人在戒斷那些資訊 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	這是完美的圖像 , 對於根本的重點 , 我們沒有人能像所有人一樣聰明地一起思考 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有一個人 , 沒有一個聯盟 , 沒有一個國家 , 沒有一個人像我們所有人一樣聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基百科的宣言很簡單:一個人人都可以自由地分享所有知識的世界 。
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我的論點是 , 藉由結合國際 , 跨部門 , 私人和公共 , 策略性的溝通 , 加起來 , 在這個21世紀 , 我們能創造出所有安全的總和 。
thank you very much . thank you . thank you .	非常感謝 。 謝謝 。 謝謝 。
